class="CollapsibleBlockContainer_3YwFL"><h2>Take Life on the Go with a Laptop</h2><div class="x-collapsibleBlock"><div class="x-collapsibleBlock-visible body_2by8a"><span width="0"><span></span><span><div><p>For life on the go, a laptop can keep up with your demands wherever you are. With the functionality of a desktop computer packed into a portable device, a laptop lets you connect to the web, watch movies, play games, edit photos and so much more. Whether you\xe2\x80\x99re looking for a standard laptop, 2 in 1 laptop or MacBook, Best Buy has a wide selection from ASUS, Microsoft, Samsung, <a href="https://m.bestbuy.ca/en-ca/collection/hp-laptops/9065">HP</a>, Toshiba and Apple to suit your needs. </p><h3>Processors</h3><p>The processor is the brain of the laptop, interpreting and performing all its commands. Intel and AMD both make processors that are tailor-made for different needs\xe2\x80\x94from basic tasks like sending emails to demanding ones like simultaneously running multiple applications. To ensure you\xe2\x80\x99ve got the right processor for your needs, consider individual specs like number of cores, overclock ability and speed. </p><h3>Screen Size and Resolution</h3><p>Size matters when it comes to laptops. A larger screen will likely make the device heavier but will give you plenty of room to work and play. A smaller screen size will make it lighter and more compact, perfect for taking on the go. Most laptops have a screen resolution of at least Full HD (1920 x 1080), and there are many options even higher resolution, even 4K! </p><h3>Family Friendly Laptops</h3><p>Many people are looking for a versatile and dependable machine that is great for the whole family. There are many great options available that offer great processing power, amazing screen resolution and responsiveness and are designed to handle a wide variety of purposes. For example, <a href="https://m.bestbuy.ca/en-ca/collection/microsoft-surface/66052">Microsoft Surface family</a> includes the tablet style Surface Pro, the Surface Laptop and the Surface Book\xe2\x80\x94there is machine to suit anyone\xe2\x80\x99s needs. For people more familiar with <a href="https://m.bestbuy.ca/en-ca/category/apple-laptops/12746015">Apple computers</a>, there are a variety of configurations, including the MacBook, MacBook Pro and MacBook Air, to ensure no matter how demanding the job, you\xe2\x80\x99ll be able to complete it on your MacBook. Your children will excel with any of these computer: Microsoft and Apple manufacture some of the best laptops for students. </p><h3>2 in 1 and Hybrid Laptops</h3><p>A 2 in 1 laptop (also called convertible or hybrid laptop) combines the functionality of a laptop with the convenience of a tablet. Equipped with both a touchscreen and a keyboard, a 2 in 1 laptop can transform from laptop to tablet in various ways\xe2\x80\x94by folding back, rotating or detaching the screen, depending on the model. A 2 in 1 is perfect when you want both a laptop and a tablet without having to buy two separate devices. If you are looking for a versatile machine, consider a Surface Pro, a Surface Laptop or a MacBook. </p><h3>Want more info about laptops?
